<script>\n        let currentGeometry = null;\n        let animationId = null;\n        let isAnimating = false;\n        \n        function toggleMenu() {\n            const menu = document.getElementById(\'menu\');\n            menu.classList.toggle(\'active\');\n        }\n        \n        function generateSacredGeometry() {\n            const name = document.getElementById(\'name\').value;\n            const birthDate = document.getElementById(\'birthDate\').value;\n            const intention = document.getElementById(\'intention\').value;\n            const style = document.getElementById(\'geometryStyle\').value;\n            const specificIntention = document.getElementById(\'specificIntention\').value;\n            \n            if (!name || !birthDate) {\n                alert(\'Please enter your name and birth date.\');\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            // Generate geometry based on birth data and intention\n            const canvas = document.getElementById(\'geometryCanvas\');\n            const ctx = canvas.getContext(\'2d\');\n            \n            // Calculate personal parameters\n            const date = new Date(birthDate);\n            const day = date.getDate();\n            const month = date.getMonth() + 1;\n            const year = date.getFullYear();\n            \n            const personalSeed = day + month + year + name.length;\n            const personalColor = `hsl(${(personalSeed * 7) % 360}, 70%, 50%)`;\n            const secondaryColor = `hsl(${(personalSeed * 13) % 360}, 60%, 40%)`;\n            \n            // Clear canvas\n            ctx.fillStyle = \'#0a0e27\';\n            ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);\n            \n            // Draw based on style\n            switch(style) {\n                case \'flower\':\n                    drawFlowerOfLife(ctx, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor);\n                    break;\n                case \'metatron\':\n                    drawMetatronsCube(ctx, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor);\n                    break;\n                case \'sri\':\n                    drawSriYantra(ctx, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor);\n                    break;\n                case \'tree\':\n                    drawTreeOfLife(ctx, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor);\n                    break;\n                case \'personal\':\n                    drawPersonalSigil(ctx, name, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor);\n                    break;\n                case \'mandala\':\n                    drawPersonalMandala(ctx, personalSeed, personalColor, secondaryColor, intention);\n                    break;\n            }\n            \n            currentGeometry = {\n                name,\n                birthDate,\n                intention,\n                style,\n                specificIntention,\n                personalSeed,\n                colors: [personalColor, secondaryColor]\n            };\n            \n            // Display insights\n            displayInsights(currentGeometry);\n            \n            // Show results\n            document.getElementById(\'results\').style.display = \'block\';\n            document.getElementById(\'results\').scrollIntoView({ behavior: \'smooth\' });\n        }\n        \n        function drawFlowerOfLife(ctx, seed, color1, color2) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            const radius = 40 + (seed % 20);\n            const circles = 7 + (seed % 6);\n            \n            ctx.strokeStyle = color1;\n            ctx.lineWidth = 2;\n            \n            // Draw central circle\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.stroke();\n            \n            // Draw surrounding circles\n            for (let i = 0; i < circles; i++) {\n                const angle = (i / circles) * Math.PI * 2;\n                const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle) * radius;\n                const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle) * radius;\n                \n                ctx.strokeStyle = i % 2 === 0 ? color1 : color2;\n                ctx.beginPath();\n                ctx.arc(x, y, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n                ctx.stroke();\n            }\n            \n            // Add inner glow\n            const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(centerX, centerY, 0, centerX, centerY, radius * 2);\n            gradient.addColorStop(0, color1 + \'33\');\n            gradient.addColorStop(1, \'transparent\');\n            ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n            ctx.fillRect(0, 0, 600, 600);\n        }\n        \n        function drawMetatronsCube(ctx, seed, color1, color2) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            const size = 100 + (seed % 50);\n            \n            ctx.strokeStyle = color1;\n            ctx.lineWidth = 2;\n            \n            // Draw outer circle\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, size, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.stroke();\n            \n            // Draw hexagon\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {\n                const angle = (i / 6) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2;\n                const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle) * size;\n                const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle) * size;\n                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);\n                else ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            }\n            ctx.closePath();\n            ctx.stroke();\n            \n            // Draw inner connections\n            ctx.strokeStyle = color2;\n            for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {\n                const angle = (i / 6) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2;\n                const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle) * size;\n                const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle) * size;\n                \n                for (let j = i + 1; j < 6; j++) {\n                    const angle2 = (j / 6) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2;\n                    const x2 = centerX + Math.cos(angle2) * size;\n                    const y2 = centerY + Math.sin(angle2) * size;\n                    \n                    ctx.beginPath();\n                    ctx.moveTo(x, y);\n                    ctx.lineTo(x2, y2);\n                    ctx.stroke();\n                }\n            }\n            \n            // Center point\n            ctx.fillStyle = color1;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, 5, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.fill();\n        }\n        \n        function drawSriYantra(ctx, seed, color1, color2) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            const layers = 4 + (seed % 3);\n            \n            ctx.strokeStyle = color1;\n            ctx.lineWidth = 2;\n            \n            // Draw concentric triangles\n            for (let layer = 0; layer < layers; layer++) {\n                const size = 200 - (layer * 40);\n                \n                // Upward triangle\n                ctx.beginPath();\n                ctx.moveTo(centerX, centerY - size);\n                ctx.lineTo(centerX - size * 0.866, centerY + size * 0.5);\n                ctx.lineTo(centerX + size * 0.866, centerY + size * 0.5);\n                ctx.closePath();\n                ctx.stroke();\n                \n                // Downward triangle\n                ctx.strokeStyle = layer % 2 === 0 ? color1 : color2;\n                ctx.beginPath();\n                ctx.moveTo(centerX, centerY + size);\n                ctx.lineTo(centerX - size * 0.866, centerY - size * 0.5);\n                ctx.lineTo(centerX + size * 0.866, centerY - size * 0.5);\n                ctx.closePath();\n                ctx.stroke();\n            }\n            \n            // Central point (bindu)\n            ctx.fillStyle = color2;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(centerX, centerY, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.fill();\n        }\n        \n        function drawTreeOfLife(ctx, seed, color1, color2) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            \n            ctx.strokeStyle = color1;\n            ctx.lineWidth = 3;\n            \n            // Draw circles (sephiroth)\n            const positions = [\n                {x: centerX, y: centerY - 120, name: "Kether"},\n                {x: centerX connections.forEach(([start, end]) => {\n                ctx.beginPath();\n                ctx.moveTo(positions[start].x, positions[start].y);\n                ctx.lineTo(positions[end].x, positions[end].y);\n                ctx.stroke();\n            });\n            \n            // Draw sephiroth\n            positions.forEach((pos, i) => {\n                ctx.fillStyle = i % 2 === \'#ffffff\';\n                ctx.font = \'10px Arial\';\n                ctx.textAlign = \'center\';\n                ctx.fillText(pos.name, pos.x, pos.y + 3);\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function drawPersonalSigil(ctx, name, seed, color1, color2) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            \n            // Create sigil from name\n            const letters = name.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z]/g, \'\').split(\'\');\n            const letterValues = letters.map(letter => letter.charCodeAt(0) - 64);\n            \n            ctx.strokeStyle = color1;\n            ctx.lineWidth = 3;\n            \n            // Draw sigil pattern\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            letterValues.forEach((value, index) => {\n                const angle = (value / 26) * Math.PI * 2 + (seed % 360) * Math.PI / 180;\n                const radius = 100 + (index * 20);\n                const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle) * radius;\n                const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle) * radius;\n                \n                if (index === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);\n                else ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            });\n            ctx.closePath();\n            ctx.stroke();\n            \n            // Add energy centers\n            ctx.fillStyle = color2;\n            letterValues.forEach((value, index) => {\n                const angle = (value / 26) * Math.PI * 2 + (seed % 360) * Math.PI / 180;\n                const radius = 100 + (index * 20);\n                const x = centerX + Math.cos(angle) * radius;\n                const y = centerY + Math.sin(angle) * radius;\n                \n                ctx.beginPath();\n                ctx.arc(x, y, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n                ctx.fill();\n            });\n  }\n        \n        function drawPersonalMandala(ctx, seed, color1, color2, intention) {\n            const centerX = 300;\n            const centerY = 300;\n            const petals = 6 + (seed %
